       <div class="widget Blog" id="Blog1">
        <div class="post">
         <h3 style="display: none">
          <a href="http://gainhappinessnow.blogspot.com/2015/03/views-of-happiness.html" title="Views of Happiness">
           Views of Happiness
          </a>
         </h3>
         <span id="p2430973014854921827">
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           What about animals, who are clearly capable of feeling pleasure and pain and who cannot respond to the "happiness question"
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Response does not have to be verbal but can be through behaviour in other forms as well
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           For example, a mouse that is staying away from the electroshock stick demonstrates that it does not want to re-live the experience of touching it
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           It is possible to set up experiments that clearly show the animal
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           * It still does not provide full transparency on how happy we are overall as we would need to run this process (asking the happiness question) for every single moment of our lives
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           s getting measured does not have to be restricted to a "short moment" (e
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           a second), but can be over a longer period of time, in the extreme case asking "would you chose to re-live your entire life again if offered (with exactly the same emotions, know-how etc
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           The risk with extending the measured period, however, is that there can be substantial distortions as our assessment of the past is very much influenced how we feel at the time we make the assessment
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           For example, if we are feeling great our assessment of our past will most likely be substantially more positive than if we just had a major stroke of fate, while there should be no difference as the life we
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           This distortion and how to deal with it will be addressed in the following posts
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Before continuing further and addressing the logical questions that result from this, I would like to stop here and ask you what you think about this "preliminary" definition
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Happiness is a well sought after emotion by all of us
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Countless products and services are offered to provide this mindset so many seek
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           In fact, most advertisements for products use happiness as the subliminal benefit
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Many believe that if they achieve a specific goal or make a certain acquisition, the feeling of happiness will belong to them
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Some believe that if they follow all the rules of their religion, it will come
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Unfortunately, this state of mind is short-lived when attached to an agenda
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Happiness is a simple or complex state of being depending on how you define it in your mind
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Let's start with the dictionary definition of happiness
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           The classic Webster defines happiness as "a state of well-being and contentment
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           " How does one achieve a "state of well-being and contentment"
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           That is the million dollar question so many seek the answer to
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           First, you have to determine what makes YOU content
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           The interesting truth about happiness is that there is no simple answer
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           The truth is that what makes one happy can make another miserable
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Take it a step further and determine what makes you content
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Bottom line, the negative energy of stress and anxiety is not dominating your mindset
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Lack of happiness can be ignited and maintained by fears of countless sources, negative foresight of the future, being unwilling to forgive events from the past and a sense of no purpose
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           True happiness is experienced when it is ignited by helping others feel the emotion of happiness
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           In fact, the more you make others happy, the happier you will be
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Just as it is true in the law of give and take, you will find what you seek when you unconditionally find a way to give it to someone else
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Another important truth to remember is that nothing is permanent
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Therefore, do not think that if happiness is not your current state of mind, it will not happen
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Without experiencing sadness or any other unhappy emotion, you cannot appreciate the positive opposite
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           When you truly feel this truth in your heart, you will use the negative experience as an opportunity to learn from and grow
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           With this practice, the happiness you will experience can become even better; in fact, it can cross the line to a state of bliss
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           As you learn to be content within your heart at the present moment, you will feel the energy of peace
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Happiness involves so much more than being satisfied
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Happiness, if adequately defined, would include the reference to peace of mind and peace in the heart
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Happiness would be defined as an active positive energy that circulates through your body
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Happiness would be defined as being content and grateful as a result of the gifts you share with others
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Simply stated, happiness would be defined as a positive energy that is within you and permeates from you
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Regardless of your circumstances, the answer is yes
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           You do not have to be rich, you do not have to be popular, you do not have to have countless possessions
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           You simply have to choose the path you want to pursue in life to make others happy and just like the blissful state of deep sleep, happiness will envelop you without you consciously realizing it
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           When you do consciously become aware of it, share it and feel it grow
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Have you ever met someone who's married or in a romantic relationship &amp; asked them how they would know their relationshipis successful
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           I have; in fact, I've been the guy asking the questions
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           It may have seemed like a misstep on my part, but really it was an intervention designed to get the group of guys I meet with to begin thinking about how they know if they're in a successful relationship
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           What this means to you is this: How will you ever know if your marriage has reached the level of success you hope it will if you have YET to define what it would look like to be successful
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Unfortunately, most people not only don't have an answer to that question, they also don't know the TRUE characteristics of a successful relationship
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           I was recently watching a episode of my new favorite TV show, "How I Met Your Mother"
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           The lead character, Ted, was talking about his "ideal" wife
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           She like tennis, dogs; wanted two kids - a boy and a girl; she was intelligent, social; liked the same favorite book, and so forth
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Finding this 'ideal' woman represented a successful relationship to him
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           I'm sure you know a lot of other people like this - they believe if they just find the 'right' person, their 'soul-mate' then they'll have the perfect relationship
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           And as you know, this couldn't be further from the truth
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Simply finding someone who shares interests as you, or who meets most of the items on your 'list', does NOT mean you will have a successful relationship
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Here's the criteria you'll want to strive towards to have a stable, successful, fulfilling &amp; passionate marriage (I'll break each of these down in a series of articles)
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Each criteria applies to BOTH you and your partner; if just one of you meets the criteria, there will definitely be a 'red flag' for you in that area
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           I'll also reveal to you some 'extenuating circumstances' which, if apply, will lessen the overall danger if one of you is lacking one of the criteria
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Secure attachment (or at least in the process of working through attachment issues), &amp; this involves:
           <span style="white-space: pre-wrap;">
           </span>
           a) Resolution of childhood losses, hurts, wounding, trauma (more on this later), &amp; deprivations
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           b) Need identification: Being able to be aware of, and meet, your own needs (especially emotionally) in healthy, effective &amp; appropriate avenues - instead of avoiding or 'checking out'
           <span style="white-space: pre-wrap;">
           </span>
           c) The ability to give &amp; receive comfort (by the way, I only know two couples, and a handful of single people, who are able to EFFECTIVELY &amp; TRULY give comfort
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">

          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Familiarity breeds contempt - so the old saying goes - and, indeed, there is considerable psychological evidence to back this up
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">

          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">

          </div>

          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           If you are looking for a potential life partner, a person who does not have that same interest as you will not be able to fulfill your dreams of a happy life
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Choose the one that is mature, responsible, and a good person
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Make sure you have common interests about your future such as marriage and children
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Also, it is a good idea to find someone with common hobbies such as someone who loves the outdoors like you do, loves animals like you do, or is easygoing like you are
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           In order to have a happy relationship, you must be able to talk about the problems that you are having in your life
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           If there is no communication in your life, you are just setting your relationship up for failure
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           If you are having second thoughts about your relationship, tell your partner
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           They may be feeling the same way and you could figure out a healthy way to work on it together
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           If your partner does something to make you angry, tell them so you can figure out a way that it will not happen again
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           If you want a happy relationship, I am sure that means you want to truly enjoy each other
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Having date nights can give you the alone time you need to be able to communicate and have fun together
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Try making date nights a priority even if they are only once a month
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           You must be able to have fun together and a good time being alone with each other if you want to be happy with them
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Even a movie night on the couch can be a date night and gives you the time you need to enjoy one another
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Although many people may think that happy relationships are impossible, they are definitely not and anyone can have one
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           If you truly want a happy relationship and do all that you can to accomplish it, it will happen
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           However, the focus should not be limited to if one obtains tangible things
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           For example, I will be happy if I get a house, a car, or a higher paying job
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           When an individual base their happiness on the &ldquo;if contingency,&rdquo; they are limiting their emotion
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           The emotion of happiness creates a positive attitude
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           When one is happy, there is a belief created that one can achieve anything
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Happiness inspires individuals to have a positive outlook on life
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Happiness becomes the priority in having a good day
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Therefore one should make it a daily practice and decide to be happy
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Affirm Your Decision to be happy and make it your top priority
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Our Mission: to spread happiness globally one person at a time
          </div>
         </span>

        <div class="post">
         <h3 style="display: none">
          <a href="http://gainhappinessnow.blogspot.com/2015/03/lines-of-happiness_10.html" title="Lines of Happiness">
           Lines of Happiness
          </a>
         </h3>
         <span id="p4653495973380077078">
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Imagine coming back from the shops and showing your shiny new happiness, to your family and friends
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Imagine taking your new happiness for a test drive
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           With your new happiness, you can handle it, and also be happy while handling it
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Never mind I can smile while sympathetically letting her unwind
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           With your Great Happiness you know that whatever happens in life you will happily handle it
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Just how much would you pay for this paradise, if you knew that for the rest of your life you could happily deal with everything that life sends your way, good or bad
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Imagine knowing that every day for the rest of your life you could happily handle anything and everything
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Imagine that you never again let fear stop you from doing what you need to do
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Bad News: The bad news is you can't go down the shops and buy Heroic or Great Happiness
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           You will find Heroic and Great Happiness right here
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Is both very easy and also hard, it is instant and a lifetime away
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Best of all is an unbreakable commitment to have this happiness come what may
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           After your decision you must follow through by sticking to it no matter what
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           You will not be pushed aside from your commitment to have this happiness
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           It is one of the most important values in your life
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Your decision to have this happiness is instant, and will remain instant every time you make this decision to be happy, every day, hour minute
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Achieving Heroic Happiness takes a lifetime of practice, and work
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           The longer you practice it the greater your happiness is for longer
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Eventually you will move from being occasionally happy, to having Great Happiness, then having that prized goal of Heroic Happiness
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Research shows that only a small percentage of people consider themselves "very happy"
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Fortunately, for most people, there is a solution - a way to get started on a path to true, complete, and life-long happiness
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           You see, the first reason we can't be completely happy is that most of us don't really know what would make us truly happy in life
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           more money, a better relationship, a more fulfilling job, better looks, having children, less stress, fewer 'problems', or whatever
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           The truth is, though, most of us don't truly know because we never take the time to really figure it out - partly because it isn't always that easy to determine exactly what we need in our life to be totally happy
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           I call it our personal Definition of Happiness ' and it is different for everyone
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           The things that make me happy (or could make me happier) are different than the things that make you happy (or could make you happier)
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           If you looked up your own personal Definition of Happiness in the dictionary, what would it say
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           In other words, what is it - exactly and specifically - that would make you totally happy in life
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           If you could name 5 or 6 things that, if you had them in your life right now, would make you totally and truly happy for the rest of your life - what would they be
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           But have you ever really sat down and thought about it
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           And that's one of the main reasons why most people CAN'T be totally happy
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           It's like wanting to live in a warm, sunny climate and thinking that Seattle is where you want to be ' because it's such a nice place
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Yes, it is a great place, but it probably wouldn't really be the right place for you
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           You would not be totally happy living there (again, even though it's a great place) since Seattle is a somewhat of a cooler, rainier city and what you really want is to live in a warm, sunny place
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           So, are you certain you know exactly what would make you totally happy in life
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Again, most people don't ' mainly because they haven't taken the time and effort to figure it out
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           And, yes, it can require time and effort (and a lot of thought)
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Most people just go through life striving to "be happy" (thinking they know what it would take to get there) but not really knowing
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           It's no wonder many people never get there (and can't be truly happy)
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           It's part of the reason why so many "famous", "wealthy", "successful", "healthy" people are miserable
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           They think the fame, wealth, success, and good health will make them happy (like thinking Seattle is the right place to live) but when they get those things they find out it's not what they really need to be happy
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           All those things are nice, and may add to a sense of contentment or joy, but it's not enough
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           It is important to know that the first essential step in the journey to the happiest possible life is to know the destination
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           That destination is described by your personal Definition of Happiness
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Once you define what happiness means for you personally, you will be in a much better position to identify the steps required to get there by creating your personal Happiness Plan ' which is your 'map' for the journey to complete and total happiness and fulfillment
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           If you need help figuring out what would truly make you happy in life, click here
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Your Definition of Happiness is not a personal mission statement or declaration of your purpose in life
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           It simply means answering the question: what would make you a totally happy and fulfilled person forever
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Stated another way, if your life were to include everything written in your personal Definition of Happiness you would be totally happy for life, regardless of the circumstances
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           As Linda Ellis put it so well in her hugely popular poem called The Dash, it's really all about how you want to live your life (you can get your own copy of The Dash by clicking here - or you can just "experience" the poem by clicking here)
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           This is about you, your values, your priorities, your passions, and your identity
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           The main requirement is that it states your true feelings and includes everything required for you to be as happy as possible
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           It is not easy for most people to define happiness for themselves
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           It takes considerable thought, honesty, reflection, and introspection
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           And, it really needs to follow a certain "formula" for it to be valid - and form the foundation for your happiness
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           For starters, it is best for your Definition of Happiness to consist of the right number of "criteria" required for your happiness
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           In other words, your definition cannot contain too many or too few of the criteria which are needed for your happiness
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           For example, if you included only one thing (one criterion) in your definition that is required for your total happiness and it doesn't work out as planned, it will be unlikely that you'll be able to be truly happy in your life
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Not only that, it is quite unlikely that anyone would have just one criterion for total happiness
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           So, if your Definition of Happiness were simply to become wealthy, for example, you would likely never be truly happy if that didn't happen for some reason
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Additionally, though, even if you did get wealthy, you would probably still not be really happy if you had terrible relationships, significant regrets, or no self-respect
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Wealth, in this example, could be part of your Definition of Happiness, but it should not be your entire definition
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           And, surely, wealth alone is very rarely (I would say never) anyone's ONLY criterion for happiness
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Similarly, if there are too many criteria for you to meet in your personal Definition of Happiness, it is difficult to get them all aligned and you will likely not achieve maximum happiness either
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           So, for example, if you truly needed wealth, fame, perfect health, good looks, many good friends, a great marriage, an active sex life, enough free time to travel 12 weeks every year, a career as a successful musician, and the freedom to spend lots of time with your children, it might be tough to be totally happy since all those criteria are not likely to be met
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           You must take the time and effort to create your own personal Definition of Happiness
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Guideline number 3 above may need a bit of explanation
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           'Relatively easy' here basically means setting yourself up for success (i
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           It doesn't necessarily mean it's a certainty, but it does mean it should be something likely to be achieved if you work on it
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Things like 'getting rich' or 'becoming one of the best, most popular musicians in the world', for example, are not easy criteria to meet
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           They take considerable effort, persistence, maybe some 'luck' and probably the help of other people
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           'Contributing regularly to the lives of others' and 'pursing personal growth', on the other hand, are relatively easy to achieve ' partly because they are almost entirely within your control
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           But, as you can see, by 'relatively easy' I don't mean it takes no time or effort ' since, as you can see in my 'easy' examples here, they definitely take focus, commitment, time, and effort as well
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Now, as you contemplate your own requirements for happiness (the 'criteria' for your Definition of Happiness), consider questions like:
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           The most critical factor in creating your personal Definition of Happiness is that it must be your definition
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           You should even feel some emotion when you read it, because once you have achieved a life totally consistent with your definition, nothing can make you unhappy, regardless of the circumstances that occur in your life, including the inevitable difficulties and challenges we all experience in life
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           So again, crafting your Definition of Happiness is a very important first step to lifelong happiness
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Key Point #1: To be as happy as possible in life, your 'Definition of Happiness' must be fulfilled as completely as possible
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Key Point #2: If you are truly happy according to your specific personal Definition of Happiness, nothing can make you unhappy ' even intensely negative situations or circumstances
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           As with many other happiness-building concepts, as mentioned previously, determining your Definition of Happiness can be difficult
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           So for additional help in creating your definition, click here
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           If you listen to the news reports, the key to happiness is to be found in a stack of dollar bills because that is how "they" all measure success and successful people are happy people, right
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           When people talk about dreams, they often speak of those dreams in terms of things that all cost money
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Once you eliminate all of the outside voices, you start to listen to the one inside of you, the voice that is telling you what you need
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Sure, you might need to work a job that leaves you less than thrilled to earn enough money to pay the bills, but do you have to stay extra hours at that miserable place if you don't like being there
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           One study looked at a group of parents who admitted that they did not care for their current job but were not in the position to make a change
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Some were asked to work overtime hours and some were not
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           The people who worked the overtime earned more money than the others but in terms of happiness were either equally as happy or less happy than those who worked fewer hours
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           The reason was simple: not only were the overtime hours cutting into free time and time spent with family, it ended up costing more to many of the parents in the long run
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Once they paid for additional child care, which sometimes meant some stressful negotiating to get the babysitter to stay late or even hiring a second care giver on a temporary basis, their overtime bonus was far lower than expected
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           If work is not doing it for you it is important to find at least one activity that makes you truly happy
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           How long has it been since you laughed until you were breathless
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           How long has it been since you took a nap for no reason or stayed up late to watch a Mel Brooks movie with your favorite person
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Only you can hear the voice inside of you that is telling you to buy a red balloon and give it to a frowning child or to dance to the music in the grocery store
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Only you know what makes you happiest and only you can get it for you
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Happiness is the key to life and it is in your own back pocket
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Have you asked yourself at times how can I be happy
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: small;">
           Do you feel that there are things stopping your happiness in life
          </div>
         </span>

         </script>

        <div class="post">
         <h3 style="display: none">
          <a href="http://gainhappinessnow.blogspot.com/2014/10/are-you-happy-at-work-is-it-them-or-you.html" title="Are you happy at work? Is it them or you? Find happiness at work">
           Are you happy at work? Is it them or you? Find happiness at work
          </a>
         </h3>
         <span id="p1215169919742188555">
          <div class="MsoNormal">
           We all face the dilemma of happiness at work. It is one the
most important factors that influence the quality of work input by an
individual. One falls in either of the two categories, first one is in
profession one always wanted to be in or one is in the profession that one
didn't expect to be in. In the first case, chances are one would findhappinessin
most cases. However, the second case is
the one most of usbelong to. Most of the people in the world are in the
profession that didn't want/plan/expect to be in. Nevertheless we should always try to keep ourselves in happiness.
          </div>
          <div class="MsoNormal">
           <br/>
          </div>
          <div class="MsoNormal">
           Now in either case, the happiness at work of an individual
is mostly always dependent on the individual and rarely on the external
factors. Most of us end up continuing working in our non-chosen field because
of life pressures/money requirement/ children or other reasons. This leads to
more frequent boredom, concentration loss and loss of happiness. We can prevent this by
           <a href="http://gainhappinessnow.blogspot.in/2014/10/the-happiness-project.html" target="_blank">
            treating ourselves
           </a>
           with little goodies every now and then like going on a vacation to maintain our happiness. This way we ensure our
happiness is on the priority list and we never fail to be happy at work.
          </div>
          <div class="MsoNormal">
           <br/>
           <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
            <tbody>
             <tr>
              <td style="text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-gSEtaUdtalY/VEdfI3VxxWI/AAAAAAAAAX0/h-_bVdMD15I/s1600/happy-people-at-work.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                <img border="0" height="294" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-gSEtaUdtalY/VEdfI3VxxWI/AAAAAAAAAX0/h-_bVdMD15I/s1600/happy-people-at-work.jpg" width="320"/>
               </a>
              </td>
             </tr>
             <tr>
              <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
               Happiness at work
              </td>
             </tr>
            </tbody>
           </table>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <br/>
          </div>
          <div class="MsoNormal">
           So many times people tend to complain that the main reason
of their unhappiness at work is the boss. It is highly imperative to have an
understanding boss who can support in times of need and maintain your levels of happiness. In fact a third of people
who leave their jobs is because attitude of their boss and loosing happiness because of him/her. Sometimes it can be
challenge to gel with a person but with a careful approach it can be done
easily. It is better to be straight forward with your boss regarding your
concerns and ensuring your happiness. If he/she doesn't address them repeatedly, its better to talk to HR
and senior management at once to resolve it so as not to loose your happiness at work. Even HR people would recognize the fact
happiness at work is very important and would help one to attain happiness.
          </div>
          <div class="MsoNormal">
           <br/>
          </div>
          <div class="MsoNormal">
           Politics at work can be very interruptive to the entire
environment and overall bonding levels between staff members and their happiness. Most of
unproductive workers are likely to be more politics oriented and find their happiness in it. There are two
ways to handle politics in office. The best way is to stay out of politics.
Just do your work and dont get involved in anyones business and any nonsense
that goes around to keep your happiness intact. Have good relations with anyone and everyone to spread happiness around you. Be sweet to people and they will be good to
you to increase happiness score. The second and more daring way is to create your own politics and be on
top of anyone else. You create the gossips, news and activities and thus be in control of your happiness. This is often done
by those who want to more up the ladder. This way you can be the star and at
the same time have people follow you and respect you and increase happiness. This creates space and
people look up to you to solve their problems and help to increase their happiness. Politics done in a good way is
good for your organization as well. Either way you will be happy as you will be
in control of yourself and the situations and have happiness at work.
          </div>
          <div class="MsoNormal">
           <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
            <tbody>
             <tr>
              <td style="text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-tMu8J4l1sC4/VEdfJx3OC4I/AAAAAAAAAX8/Qt9-4RAo4yg/s1600/workplace.happiness.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                <img border="0" height="143" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-tMu8J4l1sC4/VEdfJx3OC4I/AAAAAAAAAX8/Qt9-4RAo4yg/s1600/workplace.happiness.png" width="320"/>
               </a>
              </td>
             </tr>
             <tr>
              <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
               Happiness at work
              </td>
             </tr>
            </tbody>
           </table>
           <br/>
          </div>
          <div class="MsoNormal">
           People who are not able to perform the job at optimum levels
also face the problem of lack of happiness at work. The way out of this is to
seek others opinion on how you can be better. Its also beneficial to check the
best practices and seek your superiors help. This would enable their happiness as well as yours. Sometimes a simple demonstration by
another person is of great help. I have always followed my method. Whenever I used
to come back home, I would spend 5 minutes of time with myself thinking about
things that I could improve on the next day and what to do to improve them.
These 5 minutes always helped me to stay ahead of the game and become top
performer and get higher levels of happiness.
          </div>
          <div class="MsoNormal">
           <br/>
          </div>
          <div class="MsoNormal">
           Sometimes some people are also drama kings or drama queens.
It is highly suggested not to indulge in such tendencies and stick to the work so as not to fuck the happiness of others.
Drama at work place is not appreciated and is a total waste of time. It also
helps one to make enemies or rivals at work and reduce happiness levels of everyone around. This is a total waste of time and
effort not only for the one who does it but also for the ones around decreasing their overall happiness. There is
a total feeling of disgust which begins to affect the general moral and happiness. Usually in
such cases the person responsible for it ends up earning the wrath of the
management or the people around leading to loss of employment.
          </div>
          <div class="MsoNormal">
           <br/>
          </div>
          <div class="MsoNormal">
           There are some workplaces which involve multi-tasking and
co-operation and coordination between different departments. People often find
it tough in the beginning to adjust in such job roles, which leads to less happiness at work and dissatisfaction. One should give himself/herself more
time to adjust in the environment and also try to build
           <a href="http://gainhappinessnow.blogspot.in/2014/09/happiness-through-our-relations.html" target="_blank">
            better relationships
           </a>
           with others. Time also smoothens out things and makes it easier to adjust the
pulls and pushes thus leading to better happiness levels.
          </div>
          <div class="MsoNormal">
           <br/>
          </div>
          A lot of times much of the loss of happiness is because of delayed
rewards and recognition. Everybody who goes to work needs a little appreciation
for the efforts they put in to maintain their happiness levels. If it so happens that the recognition is being delayed
time and again then the loss of happiness creeps in. Sometimes the rewards are the
form of cash and kind. What the management may not realize is that it may be
very essential for the person in the particular month to have some extra money to keep up his happiness or the rewards are an excellent happiness booster for him.
What one can do is to inform the responsible and wait for the action. We should
also realize that so many times a lot of things are not in our hands and we
should keep calm and hope for the best to have sustained levels of happiness. Upon repeated attempts, its best
advisable to move to a employment which is more employee centric so one can have happiness at work.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <span style="line-height: 115%;">
           <span style="font-family: inherit;">
            In this article I have highlighted several
reasons and situations which can be detrimental to an employees happiness at
work and the steps one can take to correct them. However we live in the world
and almost everything is imperfect and it is
            <a href="http://gainhappinessnow.blogspot.in/2014/09/tips-to-live-life-full-of-happiness.html" target="_blank">
             our own approach
            </a>
            to happiness which makes
things perfect or not. Our happiness is much more dependent on us and not on
others. It is to do with the fact how we approach the issues, whether we take
them with cool head or we make a big issue of a trivial matter. One has to
adjust to the existing environment and culture of the workplace as it cannot
adjust to us. So its better we become the kings of our happiness.
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>

           <script src="/feeds/posts/default/1215169919742188555?alt=json-in-script&amp;callback=av">
           </script>
           <h4 class="bl_popover" data-content="Hi, My name Is Hunny Bhagya.I like CSS, but I'm a No PRO...Still Learning About It Everday!.         <div class="post">
         <h3 style="display: none">
          <a href="http://gainhappinessnow.blogspot.com/2014/10/sins-of-happiness.html" title="Sins of Happiness">
           Sins of Happiness
          </a>
         </h3>
         <span id="p4021403202570162730">
          <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
           <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-welnXhtbw_I/VB_6nJbO0qI/AAAAAAAAAEo/yqxlZWj0hEI/s1600/make-your-own-happiness.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
            <img border="0" height="213" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-welnXhtbw_I/VB_6nJbO0qI/AAAAAAAAAEo/yqxlZWj0hEI/s1600/make-your-own-happiness.jpg" width="320"/>
           </a>
          </div>
          <span style="background-color: white; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
            <br/>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
            <br/>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
            Sins of Happiness
           </span>
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="background-color: white; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
            <br/>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
            <br/>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           You may have material wealth, even power or fame, yet still be unhappy. Or you may have little more than the shoes on your feet yet overflow with joy, because happiness is a
          </span>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: white; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           state of mind
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           .
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white;">
           <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
            <span style="line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
             If you want to be truly happy,you'vegot to look to yourself because true happiness comesfrom within.
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="background-color: white;">
           <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
            <span style="line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
             <br/>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           Allow yourself to be immersed in whatever it is youre doing right now, and take time to really
          </span>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           be
           <i>
           </i>
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           in the present moment.
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           Life is too short to
          </span>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           wait
          </span>
          <em style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
          </em>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           to be happy.
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           You know what makes
          </span>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           you
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           feel good, use some
           <a href="http://gainhappinessnow.blogspot.in/2014/09/tips-to-live-life-full-of-happiness.html" target="_blank">
            simple ideas
           </a>
           to make your day a bit more joyful.
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           <br/>
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           Sins that make happiness very hard to come by -
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           <br/>
          </span>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           Comparing Yourself to Others
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           <br/>
          </span>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 0px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
            Talking About Your Dreams Instead of Going to Work on Them
           </span>
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 0px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
            <br/>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 0px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
            <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 0px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
             Listening to People With Nothing Positive to Say
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 0px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
            <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 0px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
             <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 0px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
              Focusing on the News
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           <br/>
          </span>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 0px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
            Deciding Someone Else Needs to Change
           </span>
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           <br/>
          </span>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           Thinking Happiness Is a Destination You Can Reach
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           <br/>
          </span>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 0px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
            Forgetting to Say Thank You
           </span>
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 0px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
            <br/>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 0px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
            <span style="line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
             Its easy to take for granted all that you have.
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 0px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
            <span style="line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
             <br/>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 0px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
            <span style="line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
             Avoid replaying past negative events in your head or worrying about the future.
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 0px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
            <span style="line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
             <br/>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
           <span style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 0px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
            <span style="line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
             Happiness is
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           based on worldly accomplishments.
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           <br/>
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           Don't be regretful for what you don't have.
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           <br/>
          </span>
          <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
           <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-CkcgI2QsoxQ/VCFlunh4BzI/AAAAAAAAAIo/dtuPtR5RdVw/s1600/Happiness-quotes-31056420-413-589.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
            <img border="0" height="320" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-CkcgI2QsoxQ/VCFlunh4BzI/AAAAAAAAAIo/dtuPtR5RdVw/s1600/Happiness-quotes-31056420-413-589.jpg" width="224"/>
           </a>
          </div>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           <br/>
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           These are some of our common mistakes/biases/mind blocks to happiness, which is a universal and pure feeling to which every individual has a right. It comes from very simple time moments and the maximum happiness is often a result of a trivial action such a smile of a infant or my favourite team on victory. Time has been memorial that happiness comes to those who are content and satisfied and the ones who are greedy and dishonest.
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           <br/>
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           Remove the blocks to your pathway to heaven. Yes !!
           <a href="http://gainhappinessnow.blogspot.in/2014/09/exercises-are-happiness-booster.html" target="_blank">
            Happiness is
           </a>
           the pathway to heaven and it is right here on earth for us to feel and be a part of it.
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           <br/>
          </span>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           Paritosh
          </span>
          <br/>
          <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 19.2000007629395px;">
           <br/>
